Q2996	SELECT catalog_returns.cr_return_ship_cost  FROM catalog_returns ORDER BY catalog_returns.cr_refunded_hdemo_sk ASC, catalog_returns.cr_reversed_charge ASC   LIMIT 424
Q2997	SELECT catalog_sales.cs_ship_addr_sk, customer_demographics.cd_dep_count  FROM catalog_sales FULL OUTER JOIN customer_demographics ON catalog_sales.cs_ship_cdemo_sk = customer_demographics.cd_demo_sk   LIMIT 289
Q2998	SELECT catalog_returns.cr_refunded_cdemo_sk  FROM catalog_returns ORDER BY catalog_returns.cr_reason_sk ASC, catalog_returns.cr_store_credit ASC   LIMIT 225
Q2999	SELECT catalog_returns.cr_refunded_addr_sk, max(distinct(catalog_returns.cr_returned_time_sk)) AS c_11, sum(catalog_returns.cr_return_amount) AS c_12  FROM catalog_returns GROUP BY catalog_returns.cr_refunded_addr_sk   LIMIT 196
Q3000	SELECT min(web_returns.wr_refunded_addr_sk) AS c_10, max(distinct(web_returns.wr_returning_hdemo_sk)) AS c_11, max(distinct(web_returns.wr_returned_time_sk)) AS c_12  FROM web_returns GROUP BY web_returns.wr_order_number, web_returns.wr_returning_customer_sk   LIMIT 196
